shared_focus = {
	id = KIR_focus_1
	icon = GFX_goal_KIR_kiria_1007
	x = 8
	y = 0

	cost = 2.9

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_bipartite_war_started_flag
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = KIR_bipartite_war_tt
				always = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus KIR_focus_1"
		country_event = { id = kirin.1 hours = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_begins_plenum_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_gain_plenum_modifier_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_PP_var value = 0.05 }
			set_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_stab_var value = 0 }
			set_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_DD_var value = 0 }
			set_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_democratic_var value = 0.1 }
			set_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_fascism_var value = 0.1 }
			set_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_communism_var value = 0 }
			set_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_neutrality_var value = 0.1 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIR_plenum_dynamic_modifier }
		}
	}
}

	icon = GFX_goal_KIR_angery
	relative_position_id = KIR_focus_8c
	x = 1
	y = 1

	cost = 2.9
	
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.149
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = KIR_early_game_focus_stab_req_tt
				NOT = {
					has_stability < 0.149
				}
			}
		}
	}

	prerequisite = {
		focus = KIR_focus_8c
		focus = KIR_focus_8d
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_bipartite_war_started_flag
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = KIR_bipartite_war_tt
				always = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus KIR_focus_9e"
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_modify_silence_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_silence_experience1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = KIR_the_silence_experience_gain_var value = 0.1 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_silence_planning2_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = KIR_the_silence_planning_var value = 0.10 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_silence_training1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { var = KIR_the_silence_training_var value = 0.1 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_silence_attrition1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { var = KIR_the_silence_attrition_var value = 0.2 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_silence_organisation1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = KIR_the_silence_army_org_var value = 0.2 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
		unlock_decision_tooltip = KIR_support_decision_1
		unlock_decision_tooltip = KIR_support_decision_2
		unlock_decision_tooltip = KIR_support_decision_3
		unlock_decision_tooltip = KIR_support_decision_4
		unlock_decision_tooltip = KIR_support_decision_5
	}
}

shared_focus = {

	icon = GFX_goal_KIR_drinking

	x = 0
	y = 2

	cost = 2.9

			}

				tooltip = KIR_early_game_focus_stab_req_tt
				NOT = {
					has_stability < 0.149
				}
			}
		}
	}

	prerequisite = {
		focus = KIR_focus_7g
	}
	
	bypass = {
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = equestrian_civil_war
			EQS = {
				OR = {
					exists = no
					is_subject = yes
					has_capitulated = yes
					has_civil_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_bipartite_war_started_flag
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = KIR_bipartite_war_tt
				always = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	completion_reward = {

		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_unlock_entry_fickle_current
		add_to_variable = { KIR_diary_SG_protag_3_button_var = 1 }
		meta_effect = {
		  text = {
			set_variable = { KIR_diary_SG_protag_3_entry_[IDKIRX]_var = 203 } 
			set_variable = { KIRDiary3Entry[IDKIRX]TitleVar = 203 }
		  }
		  IDKIRX = "[?KIR_diary_SG_protag_3_button_var|0]"
		}
		KIR_unlock_entry_effect = yes
		KIR_diary_SG_protag_3_button_click_effect = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = navdoctrine_bonus
			bonus = 2
			uses = 1
			category = naval_equipment
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = EQS
			modifier = KIR_equestrian_naval_trade
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_we_will_have_equestrian_naval_blueprints_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					not = { has_dlc = "Man the Guns" }
				}
				set_technology = {
					transport = 1
					early_destroyer = 1
					early_light_cruiser = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
				set_technology = {
					mtg_transport = 1
					early_ship_hull_light = 1
					early_ship_hull_cruiser = 1
					basic_battery = 1
					basic_light_battery = 1
					basic_medium_battery = 1
					basic_heavy_battery = 1
					basic_torpedo = 1
					basic_secondary_battery = 1
					basic_fire_control_system = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

shared_focus = {
	id = KIR_council_focus_treasury
	icon = GFX_goal_KIR_treasury
	relative_position_id = KIR_council_focus_1
	x = 2
	y = 2

	cost = 4.3

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = KIR_council_focus_2a
		focus = KIR_council_focus_2b
	}
	
	offset = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = KIS_council_salvation_front_civil_war_scenario
		}
		x = 2
		y = 0
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus KIR_council_focus_treasury"
		country_event = { id = kirin_council.7 hours = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_council_focus_treasury_tt
		set_country_flag = KIS_unlocked_treasury
		#####################
		## Treasury Wealth ##
		#####################
		#set_variable = { var = TreasuryWealth value = 0 }
		###################
		## Treasury Debt ##
		###################
		set_variable = { var = TreasuryDebt value = 0 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_debt_PP_var value = 0 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_debt_consumer_goods_var value = 0 }
		##################################
		## Base Income per Factory Type ##
		##################################
		set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomePerFC value = 550 }
		set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomePerFM value = 500 }
		set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomePerFD value = 525 }
		#################################################
		## Calculate Monthly Income vis-a-vis Industry ##
		#################################################
		set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFC value = KIS.num_of_civilian_factories }
		multiply_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFC value = KISTreasuryIncomePerFC }
		set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFM value = KIS.num_of_military_factories }
		multiply_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFM value = KISTreasuryIncomePerFM }
		set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFD value = KIS.num_of_naval_factories }
		multiply_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFD value = KISTreasuryIncomePerFD }
		set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = 0 }
		add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = KISTreasuryIncomeFC }
		add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = KISTreasuryIncomeFM }
		add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = KISTreasuryIncomeFD }
		set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomePredicted value = TreasuryIncome }
		#############################################################
		## Set Last Month's Income and Variable for Monthly Change ##
		#############################################################
		set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeMonthBefore value = 0 }
		set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeChange value = 0 }
		#######################
		## Accounting Errors ##
		#######################
		set_variable = { var = TreasuryAccountingError value = 0.1 }
		#############################
		## Set Debt Penalty Ratios ##
		#############################
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_debt_PP_RATIO_var value = 250000 } ## For every 5k in debt, -2% PP factor
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_debt_PP_RATIO_var_DISPLAY value = 2 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_debt_consumer_goods_RATIO_var value = 500000 } ## For every 5k in debt, +1% consumer goods factor
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_debt_consumer_goods_RATIO_var_DISPLAY value = 1 }
		######################
		## Determine Prices ##
		######################
		KIS_treasury_figure_out_prices = yes
		set_variable = { var = KIS_fund_recruiting_cost value = 3500 }
		###################
		## 25PP per Loan ##
		###################
		set_variable = { var = KIS_take_out_loan_decision_cost value = 25 }
		#################
		## Investments ##
		#################
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_civ_factory_investment_var value = 0 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_mil_factory_investment_var value = 0 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_nav_dockyard_investment_var value = 0 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_invest_mil_fac_cost value = 9500 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_invest_civ_fac_cost value = 10000 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_invest_nav_dock_cost value = 9000 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_invest_mil_fac_days value = 180 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_invest_civ_fac_days value = 180 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_invest_nav_dock_days value = 180 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_mil_factory_maximum_capacity_var value = 50 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_civ_factory_maximum_capacity_var value = 75 }
		set_variable = { var = KIS_treasury_nav_dockyard_maximum_capacity_var value = 50 }
		hidden_effect = {
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIS_factory_donations_modifier }
		}
		### Research Slot Progress ###
		set_variable = { KIS_fund_research_decision_slot_progress_var = 10 }
	}
}

			distribution = uniform
			min = 0.1
			max = 0.15
		}
		set_variable = { var = KIS_plebiscite_verdant_fields_support_var value = KIS_plebiscite_verdant_fields_starting_support_var_TEMP }
		##Apricot Glen
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = KIS_plebiscite_apricot_glen_starting_support_var_TEMP
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0.05
			max = 0.1
		}
		set_variable = { var = KIS_plebiscite_apricot_glen_support_var value = KIS_plebiscite_apricot_glen_starting_support_var_TEMP }
		KIS_plebiscite_calculate_average_popular_support = yes
	}
}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = gwtank
				has_tech = basic_light_tank
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = tank_research
				bonus = 2.5
				uses = 1
				category = cat_light_armor
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = light_tank_equipment_1 amount = 120 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = gwtank
				NOT = {
					has_tech = basic_light_tank
				}
			}
			set_technology = { basic_light_tank = 1 }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = light_tank_equipment_1 amount = 120 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_tech = gwtank
				}
			}
			set_technology = { gwtank = 1 }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = gw_tank_equipment amount = 120 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_council_mil_focus_6_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Light Armour Regiment"
				division_names_group = KIS_infantry_regiment 
				regiments = {
					light_armor = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					light_armor = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					motorized = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					motorized = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					motorized = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					motorized = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				}
				support = {
					artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				}
				priority = 2
			}
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = { division = "name = \"No. 1 Armour Regiment 'North Steel'\" division_template = \"Light Armour Regiment\" start_equipment_factor = 1 start_experience_factor = 0.4" owner = ROOT }
				create_unit = { division = "name = \"No. 2 Armour Regiment 'North Wind'\" division_template = \"Light Armour Regiment\" start_equipment_factor = 0.7 start_experience_factor = 0.25" owner = ROOT }

			add_country_leader_trait = KIR_popular_mandate
			remove_country_leader_trait = KIR_fledgling_government
		}
	}
}
